 jab bhi is agenda par aage badhate hue vah karnataka yaa upi ke bemail gathjod kii baat karti, uske saamne pidipi ke saath gathjod kaa sawaal rakh diya jaataa
 She could neither support the accused of Kathua nor demand removal of Article 370 while joining the government
 ulte agar mahabuuba apni nitiyon par adi rahati to bijepi ke liye kashmir par naram rukh baratna lajimi hota jiske baad phir vah apane sahyogi sanghathanon ke bheetar bhi aalochana jhelti
 Mehbooba may have also breathed a sigh of relief from the bjp's backing, which felt that she was choking along with the BJP
 to ab 2019 main bijepi phir se kashmir kaa raag chhedegi
 Apart from cow protection, love jihad, triple talaq and terrorism, Kashmir will be the fourth issue on which BJP will seek votes

 The political solution of Kashmir is a question, restoring its sociality has become a much bigger challenge
 tippaniyan Today, Kashmir is the name of a body that aches with pain
 uske bheetar sautelepan kaa ek chatpataata ehsaas he

 jis sangharsh-viraam ko lekar aakiri asahmati mahabuuba sarkaar ke bheetar rahi, usee se vah malaham mil saktaa tha
 Unfortunately, the people who are snatching this ointment are forcing India's generally disciplined army to become villains in Kashmir - after all, the army's long-term presence in any society creates fear, boredom and ultimately hatred

 The film Sanjay Kak mentioned above is more than a decade old
 jaahir he, in varshon main tasviir or bhayaavah hui he
 Now the question in Kashmir is not about human rights abuses or the abolition of terrorism, where the challenge is to get Kashmir out of the mindset of an ongoing war, there is a renewed difficulty in restoring democracy
 is chunauti ko bhuulakar bijepi ne rajya sarkaar se naata todane or vahaan rajyapal shashan lagu karne kaa faisalaa kiya
 All the reasons he gave for this decision were also present in 2014, when the BJP-PDP together formed the government
 avishvaas kii khaaiyaan tab bhi itani hi gahari thim jitani aaj hai
 But then the BJP had to expand its national reach
 vah is gathjod ke zarie sabit kar rahi thi ki bijepi jammu-kashmir tak main shashan kar rahi he jo lagbhag naammumkin mana jaataa tha
 In fact, Kashmir has been just a geography for the BJP, which it has been describing as an integral part of India
 jis kashmiriat kii baat pichley dinon rajnath singh ne kii, uske prati bijepi main jaraa bhi samvedansheeltaa hoti to is behad najuk mode par vah sarkaar giraane kaa kaam nahin karti
 But Kashmir is a political issue for him which is useful in Bihar and UP elections
 anuchhed 370 (jise bijepi dhara 370 bataaya karti he) kii samaj ho yaa na ho, lekin ise hataane kii maang bijepi kaaryakartaaon kii baari lokapriy maang he
 Actually, this decision of 2018 is the beginning of 2019 preparations for BJP
 2019 main bijepi jis hindutv ke agenda ko aage badhanaa chaahati he, uski raah main ek roda kashmir bhi tha or mahabuuba se uski dosti bhi thi
 Whenever moving forward on this agenda, she would talk about mismatched alliances of Karnataka or UP, the question of alliances with PDP would be put in front of her
 vah sarkaar main shaamil rahete na kathua ke aropiyon kaa saath de sakati thi or na hi anuchhed 370 hataane kii maang kar sakati thi
 On the contrary, if Mehbooba had remained adamant on her policies, it would have been necessary for the BJP to take a soft stance on Kashmir, after which it would also face criticism within its allied organizations
 bijepi kii samarthan vaapasi se mahabuuba ne bhi shaayad raahat kii saans lee jo lagaataar yah mahasoos kar rahi thi ki bijepi ke saath se uskaa dam ghut rahaa he
 So now in 2019, BJP will again raise the tone of Kashmir
 goraksha, lav jehad, teen talaak or aatankwaad ke alaava kashmir vah chauthaa mudda hoga jis par bijepi vot maangegi
 But who will worry about Kashmir? Only the liberal elements of Kashmir will have to do this
 kashmir kaa raajnneetik hal ek sawaal he, uski saamaajikta behaal karnaa kahin zyaada badi chunauti ban gaya he
 The comments aaj kashmir dard se anthti ek deh kaa naam he
 There is a palpable feeling of steplessness within him
 uskaa ilaaj sena kii surgery nahin he, iskaa ilaaj bharose kaa malaham he
 The cease-fire with which the last disagreement remained within the Mehbooba government, could be met with that ointment
 durbhaagya se jo log yah malaham chin rahe hai, vahi bharat kii aam taur par anushaasit maani jane vaali sena ko bhi kashmir main khalanaayak banane ko majaboor kar rahe hai- aakhir kisi bhi samaaj main sena kii dirghakaalin maujuudagi dar, ub or antat nafrat hi paidaa kar sakati he
 Then when the army goes into such a difficult area, then it is very possible that not only terrorists but some common people will come in the grip of its action and eventually it will spoil the atmosphere as usual
 lekin kashmir main aman or malaham kaa sawaal sirf kashmir kaa nahin, us puure bharat kaa sawaal he jo loktantric chetana or maanviya garima main bharosa karata he
 If Kashmir does not survive with its natural humanity, it will soon have an impact on the rest of India as well
 hinsa ko asardaar hathiyaar maanane vaali sattayen duusare ilaaqon main bhi iske prayog se hichakengi nahin
 Therefore, the battle of Aman in Kashmir is the battle of the whole of India
 ise shabdadambaron se aage jaakar ladanaa hoga

 twitter
 com / 3ysc3ftmdz — ANI (@ani_news) June 13, 2017 According to school rules, children were not wearing uniforms, due to which they were punished

 bacchon ko sajaa kii ghatana sisitivi footage main record he

 haalanki ab sawaal uth rahe hai ki skool kisi vidhyaarthee ke saath aisa bartaav kaise kar saktaa he
 Most of the time of working people is spent in office
 aise main agar vahaan kaa maahaul or bos acha na ho to aap depressant kaa shikaar ho sakate hai
 This affects not only your functioning but also your mental state
 har vakt rokane-tokane vaale bos ke saath kaam karne main kaaphi dikkatein aati hai
 Leaving a job is not a solution to deal with these situations because you may face a similar boss in another office
 baharhaal, is duniya main aisi koi samasya nahin jiskaa samaadhaan maujuud na ho
 All that is needed is to take care of some things
 aap in tips kii madad se apane bos se nipat sakate hai:1
 If your boss is bothering you a lot, then first try to know whether you are falling prey to office politics
 offis main zyaadaatar samasya isi kaaran se aati he
 If this is happening due to office politics then talk to your boss as soon as possible and clear their misconceptions
 2
 You go to work, not to complain to anyone and to show weakness
 offis main bas apane kaam se matlab rakhen
 Maintain good behavior with your colleagues, but if you talk to them about work, it will be better
 3
 If the boss directly gives you any work, then complete it as soon as possible
 hameshaa apni ore se behatar kaam karne kii koshish karen taaki bos ko bevajaah shikaayat karne kaa mauka hi na mili
 4
 agar bos aapaki baat nahin sun rahaa he to ek mail likhakar apni baat kah den
 Many times it happens that the boss feels that you are also making a mistake and also retaliating
 is sthiti se bachane ke liye mail bhejnaa aasaan upaay he kyonki agar mail par anprofeshnal tareeke se koi jawaab aata he to aapke paas uskaa record rahegaa
 5
 bahes karne or gussa dikhaane se behatar he ki shanti se baat kii jaae
 It may be that talking angrily worsens rather than becoming talk and you have to bear the brunt of it
 isliye apni baat kahen lekin samajhadaari or shanti se
 6
 agar baat kuch zyada bighad gai ho jise sanbhaalanaa aapke liye mushkil he to aise main aap apane sahyogiyon kii madad le sakate hai
 Apart from colleagues, you should see who is close to the boss in the office, try to convince them and explain your situation

 gujarat main ek baar phir dalit vyakti kii hatya kaa maamla saamne aayaa he
 Here, 6 people were beaten to death by the husband of Dalit sarpanch passing through ranpur-barwala road
 ye maamla buudhvaar kaa hi he
 51-year-old Manjibhai Solanki was hit by people so much that he was badly injured, after which Manjibhai gave this information by calling someone but later succumbed
 phone par hi manjibhai ne bataaya ki unki motorcycle ko ek gaadi ne takkar maar di, uske baad 5-6 log aae or unke saath marpet kii
 People beat him with sticks
 manjibhai, ranpur taluka ke jalia gaanv kii sarpanch gita solanki ke pati hai
 When Solanki was rushed to the Civil Hospital in Ahmedabad, doctors declared him dead
 soshal media par is ghatana kaa ek video bhi viral ho rahaa he, jisamen manjibhai solanki sadak par ghayal avasthaa main pade hue hai
 And his relatives are trying to take him to the hospital
 isi video main vah khud kah rahe hai, ‘jab vah motorcycle par ja rahe the, tab ek gaadi ne unhen takkar maar di
 Later 5-6 people beat him with sticks
 ’bataa den ki pichley saal manjibhai solanki or unki patni ne police se suraksha dene kii maang kii thi
 In which he said that some people of the Kathi Darbar community (OBC) can harm him
 2018 june main unhone is masale par rajya ke lau and order dijipi ko chitthee bhi likhi gai thi
 In which he claimed that his family is in danger of being killed, which is why he needs police protection
 haalanki, unhone likhaa tha ki do maheene ke liye unhen police suraksha mili thi lekin baad main chin lee gai
 In the 46th match of the eighth edition of the Indian Premier League (IPL) at the Wankhede Stadium on Sunday, Royal Challengers Bangalore explosive batsman AB de Villiers (133 not out) along with captain Virat Kohli (82 not out) made the biggest partnership in T20 cricket in the world
 Recorded
 divilliars ne ipel-8 kaa sabase bada vyaktigat score banane ke alaava kohli ke saath duusare wicket ke liye 215 ranon kii naabad saajhedaari nibhaai
 It is the biggest partnership for any wicket and in runs in T20 cricket
 isse pehle tii-20 cricket main sabase badi saajhedaari kaa record ipel ke hi chauthe sanskaran main kings ilevan punjab ke liye adam gilcrist or shaun marsh kii jodi ne 206 ranon kii saajhedaari kar kaayam kiya tha
 Justifying the captain Virat Kohli's decision to pick the batting by winning the toss against Mumbai Indians, de Villiers played a stormy innings of 133 off 59 balls and remained unbeaten till the end
